In fact, the only requirement that is needed is what most students would already have with them – A Smartphone\r\n\r\nAll the student needed is to download the Free Blicker Student App on their Smart Phone or on their Windows 10 devices. The app uses the new Bluetooth Low Energy Technology to transmit small data packets containing the student selected responses into the air. As there is no setup or any internet connectivity needed, all the student would need to response is to tap on their desired responses and the Blicker Teacher App will immediately show all the consolidated results in a simple bar chart. \r\n\r\nThere is absolutely no need for any internet or sign up\r\n\r\nIn the Anonymous Mode, the students will feel at ease to know that his responses remains anonymous. \r\n\r\nIn the Identity Mode, the student's unique Identity will be sent along with his/her response. The teacher will then be able to know individual student's response to the questions. The teacher can also make use of Blicker to take class attendance.\r\n\r\nIn the Attendance Mode, the teacher can now automate the attendance marking with timestamp recorded and even export to an excel file. \r\n\r\nIn the Team Challenge Mode, the teacher can now split the class into teams and allow the students to work together and compete against othe teams. There is NO NEED for any cumbersome Bluetooth pairing with the Blicker Teacher App. As Bluetooth Low Energy technology is being used, this app actually consumes very low energy. Despite this, the technology allows the Blicker Student App and the Blicker Teacher App to be as far as 75 meters apart. Also, technically, the Blicker Teacher App is capable to consolidate results from hundreds of Blicker Student
